Door -                                    "Clear to open" (as required)        (LM, P)
                                          "Paratroop door/Ramp and               (LM)
                                          door opened and locked
                                          loadmaster"
             WARNING:
If an air deflector door fails to open,
do not open the respective
paratroop door and notify the pilot.
            WARNING:
Only the loadmaster(s) will open
the paratroop doors. After opening
and locking, install the safety pin.
AFI11-2MC-130V3 22 DECEMBER 2011                                             267



             WARNING:
 Crews may open either the
 paratroop doors or Ramp and door.
 Paratroop doors and Ramp and door
 will not be opened simultaneously.
                NOTE:

 and right paratroop doors. Certain
 mission requirements may dictate
 the use of the ramp and door.

specific employment procedures.

PERSONNEL AIDROP EMERGENCY PROCEDURES, PARATROOP DOOR EXIT
1. Jumpmaster                          Notified/Stop Remaining
                                       Parachutists
2. Crew Notified                       ―Towed parachutist‖                             (LM)
3. Red Lights/NVG Airdrop              Checked On
Caution Lights
4. Crew Notified                       ―Indicates                                      (LM)
                                       Conscious/Unconscious‖ or
                                       ―Parachutist released‖

                NOTE:
The jumpmaster/safety will
determine how the parachutist is
entangled. If being towed by
anything other than the static line,
the jumpmaster will attempt to free
the parachutist. If being towed by
the static line, the jumpmaster/
safety will recommend whether to
AFI11-2MC-130V3 22 DECEMBER 2011                                         315


 retrieve or cut free. If all
 parachutists have exited and no
 safety is on board, this
 responsibility rests with the
 loadmaster.
                   NOTE:
 The parachutist will indicate
 consciousness and that a reserve
 parachute is ready by maintaining a
 tight body position with both hands
 on the reserve.
 5. Static Line                         Cut on Command
                   NOTE:
 If the decision is to retieve follow
 the procedures below
             WARNING:
 The first priority is to retrieve,
 whether the parachutist is conscious
 or unconscious. If the parachutist
 cannot be retrieved and indicates
 consciousness, the parachutist will
 be cut free.

 a. Retrieval assist strap              Installed around static lines
                   NOTE:
 Ensure quick snap fittings are re-
 connected between ―A‖ frame
 center anchor cable support and
 anchor cable stop at FS 770 on
 outboard anchor cable
 b. Sling Assembly                      Installed around parachutist
                                        static line(s)
                   NOTE:
 Pull sling loop tight with retrieval
 sling hook
 c. Jump Platform                       Folded in
 d. Static lines                        Retrieve through RAS (Roller
                                        System)
 e. Retrieval                           Stopped when the cotton sleeve
                                        at the apex of the D-bags
316                                                   AFI11-2MC-130V3 22 DECEMBER 2011


                                          begins to pass through the RAS
            WARNING:
All personnel should remain clear
of the paratroop door and the line of
travel of the static line retriever
cable until the parachutist had been
retrieved to the door.

            WARNING:
During retrieval attepts ensure the
parachutist does not slip back at any
time. This does not preclude
unwinding the static line retriever to
reset the slip clutch, if necessary.
               NOTE:
It may be necessary to stop retrieval
to manually pull the D-bags through
the retriever assist strap (RAS)

               NOTE:
If TPRS is not available follow
these procedures to utilize a 5000lb
strap:
a. 5000lb Strap                           Installed
               NOTE:
Install 5000lb tiedown strap across
the paratroop door by threading the
hook end of the strap behind the
one-inch tubular brace located at FS
737, across the door under all static
lines, and behind the one-inch
tubular brace at FS 700. Hook the
hook end forward of FS 700 and
hook the ratchet end aft of FS 737.
Push the static lines to the top of the
paratroop door and remove
additional slack in the tiedown strap
by using the ratchet.
            WARNING:
Use extreme caution when routing
the 5000lb strap over the oxygen
AFI11-2MC-130V3 22 DECEMBER 2011                                            317


 regulators located at FS 740 left and
 right side.
 b. Jump Platforms                        Folded in
 c. Static Lines                          Retrieve Static Lines over
                                          5000lb Strap
             WARNING:
 All personnel should remain clear
 of the paratroop door and line of
 travel of the static line retriever
 cable until the parachutist has been
 retrieved into the door.
                  NOTE:
 It may be necessary to stop retrieval
 to manually pull the D-bags over
 the 5000lb strap.
             WARNING:
 During retrieval attepts ensure the
 parachutist does not slip back at any
 time. This does not preclude
 unwinding the static line retriever to
 reset the slip clutch, if necessary.
 d. Retrieval                             Stopped when the cotton sleeve
                                          at the apex of the D-bags
                                          begins to pass over the 5000lb
                                          strap
 6. Parachutist                           Brought into aircraft by hand
                  NOTE:
 Once the parachutist is in the door
 area and is being controlled, slightly
 unwind the retriever so the
 parachutist may be brought into the
 aircraft. The jump platform may be
 extended once the parachutist is in
 the door area to assist in retrieval.

 HIGH ALTITUDE EMERGENCY PROCEDURES FOR DECOMPRESSION
318                                                 AFI11-2MC-130V3 22 DECEMBER 2011


 SICKNESS OR UNUSUAL PAIN
 1. Crew Notified                       Provide a brief description of
                                        problem
               NOTE:
 Ensure the affected personnel
 remain on 100% oxygen until
 evaluated by a flight surgeon or
 competent medical authority.
 2. Descent and Pressurization          (As required)
               NOTE:
 Descent and/or pressurization will
 be determined by the type and
 degree of the problem.
 3. Mission                             Abort
               NOTE:
 Proceed to a location where
 qualified medical assistance is
 available. Notify the appropriate
 command and control agencies of
 the emergency. If required, request
 medical support meet the aircraft
 upon landing.

                NOTE:

1. Static Line Retriever               Rewound (as required)
2. Loose Equipment                     Stowed
3. Cargo Compartment                   Secured
PERSONNEL AIRDROP EMERGENCY PROCEDURES RAMP AND DOOR EXIT
1. Jumpmaster Notified Stop Remaining Parachutists
2. Crew Notified                       ―Towed parachutists‖                            (LM)
3. Red Light                           Checked On
4. Crew Notified                        ―Indicates                                     (LM)
                                       conscious/Unconscious‖ or
                                       ―Parachutists released‖
AFI11-2MC-130V3 22 DECEMBER 2011                          323


                  NOTE:
 The jumpmaster/safety will
 determine how the parachutist is
 entangled. If being towed by
 anything other than the static line,
 the jumpmaster will attempt to free
 the parachutist. If being towed by
 the static line, the jumpmaster/
 safety will recommend whether to
 retrieve or cut free. If all
 parachutists have exited and no
 safety is on board, this
 responsibility rests with the
 loadmaster.
                  NOTE:
 The parachutist will indicate
 consciousness and that a reserve
 parachute is ready by maintaining a
 tight body position with both hands
 on the reserve.
 5. Static Line                          Cut on Command
                  NOTE:
 It will be necessary to partially
 rewind the retriever cable to reach
 the static line for cutting
             WARNING:
 First priority is to cut the
 parachutist free if the parachutist
 indicated consciousness. If the
 parachutist is unconscious, does not
 signal, cannot be observed, or a
 condition exists that prevents
 cutting the static line, implement
 emergency retrieval procedures.
                  NOTE:
 If the decision is to retrieve follow
 the procedures below
 a. 5000lb Strap                         Installed
                  NOTE:
 To retrieve a parachutist over the
 aircraft ramp, the loadmaster will
324                                                  AFI11-2MC-130V3 22 DECEMBER 2011


install a 5000lb strap to the
emergency retrieval rings or
HSLLADS rings located at
approximately FS 848. Attach the
hook end of the strap on the ring
closest to the static line with the
hook facing forward on the
emergency retrieval rings/down on
the HSLLADS rings and attach the
ratchet end on the other side. Using
the static line retriever, the static
lines will be retrieved over the strap
and the parachutist will be brought
in by hand.
b. Static lines                          Retrieve static line(s) over the
                                         5000lb strap
            WARNING:
During retrieval attempts ensure the
parachutist does not slip back at any
time. This does not preclude
unwinding the static line retriever to
reset the slip clutch, if necessary.
            WARNING:
The last five feet are the most
crucial for the fouled parachutist. A
wildly oscillating parachutist
usually strikes the aircraft ramp
headfirst. If the parachutist is
oscillating violently, it may become
necessary to stop the retrieval
momentarily, allowing the
parachutist to stabilize, then
continue with the retrieval.
                  NOTE:
Once the parachutist is pulled up
into the ramp and is being
controlled, slightly unwind the
retriever cable so the parachutist
may be brought into the aircraft.

6. Status of Parachutist                 ―Released/Cut Away‖                    (LM)
                                         ―Malfunction checklist                 (LM)
7.                                       complete‖
AFI11-2MC-130V3 22 DECEMBER 2011                                                    325

5. Ten-minute Checklist                ―Complete‖                            (LM, E)
SIX-MINUTE
The ―Crew, six-minute warning‖ will initiate this checklist.
1. Six-minute Warning                  ―Acknowledged‖                           (LM)
2. Tail Fuse Switch                    On
3. All Personnel                       Forward of Load
4. Simul Open Handle                   Safety Pin Removed
5. Left Rail Locks                     Sequentially unlock platform
                                       for this pass
―Six-Minute Checklist Complete‖                                                 (LM)
SLOWDOWN
The ―Slowdown now‖ call will initiate this checklist.
1. Aft Anchor Cable Support Arms       Up
2. Ramp and Door Area                  Clear
3. Ramp and Door                       ―Clear to open‖                       (LM, P)
                                       ―Open and locked‖                        (LM)
AFI11-2MC-130V3 22 DECEMBER 2011                                                             359


 Check cargo door and ramp fully open, with cargo door locked in the up position and flags
 visible (when possible).
 5. Aft Anchor Cable Supports              Lowered (as required)
 6. Slowdown Checklist                     ―Complete‖                                 (LM, E)
              WARNING:
 From this point on, if the airdrop is
 aborted, or a ―NO-DROP‖ situation
 occurs, the loadmaster will
 acknowledge ―NO-DROP‖, raise
 the aft anchor cable supports (as
 required), clear the ramp and door
 to close, restrain the load(s), replace
 nose fuse safety clip, and perform
 the ―Completion of Drop
 Checklist‖. If the drop is to be
 reattempted, the airdrop checklist will
 be reinitiated beginning with the
 Twenty-Minute Checklist.

 3. ―One-minute Checklist Complete‖                                                      (LM)

 1. Extraction Parachute Manual            Pulled (as required)
 Release Handle
                 NOTE:
 If the release mechanism fails to
 release electrically, pull the manual
 release handle after hearing and
 seeing the green light illuminate.
 2. Right Rail Control Handle              EMERGENCY Position (as
                                           required)
              WARNING:
 If a platform fails to extract and the
 extraction parachute(s) are fully
 deployed, for single and sequential
 heavy equipment platforms, pull the
 right hand control handle to the
 EMERGENCY position.

checklist may be delayed until after
